)@@G@@        . YES, SET FIRST TIME KEY   @E@@@9          PCT$      BUFFER,5  OF
)@@G@@        . GET PART OF PCT     @F@@@9          L,S2      A0,BUFFER+4     OG
)@@G@@  . IF RUN PRIVILEGED, SET KEY@ @@@9          TEP,U     A0,040    @^@@@9OH
)@@G@@          SP1       PRIV@G@9@8          CSF$      USE,NUSE1         . '@OI
)@@G@@USE MASTER,SYS$*SYSTEM$LOG$'  @H@@@8          FACIL$    FACPKT          OJ
)@@G@@  . IS THERE A LOG FILE ASSIGNED ALREADY? @F@@@8          TNZ,S1    FACPOK
)@@G@@KT+6          . IF FILE NOT PRE-ASSIGNED, @H@9@8          J         CONTOL
)@@G@@0             .     GO TO REAL MASTER LOG FILE LOGIC  @H@/@9          J OM
)@@G@@        CONT0             .     GO TO REAL MASTER LOG FILE LOGIC  @H@@@/ON
)@@G@@          J         CONT1             .     GO TO REAL MASTER LOG FILE LOO
)@@G@@OGIC  @F@9@8          S         A0,PREASG         . FILE PRE-ASSIGNED, SOP
)@@G@@ET KEY@F@@@9          SP1       PREASG            . FILE PRE-ASSIGNED, SOQ
)@@G@@ET KEY@F@9@8          J         CONT1             . SKIP NEXT CYCLE LOGIOR
)@@G@@C     @F@@@9          J         CONT2             . SKIP NEXT CYCLE LOGIOS
)@@G@@C     @E@;@9CONT0     E$DIT     EPKT              . GENERATE USE IMAGE  OT
)@@G@@@^@;@9          E$MSG     USE @D@;@9          E$DECV    0,,U            OU
)@@G@@  . PRESENT CYCLE @#@;@9          E$MSGR  @G@;@9          CSF$      BUFFOV
)@@G@@ER+28,14      . '@USE LOG$,SYS$*SYSTEM$LOG$(0)' @D@;@9          CSF$    OW
)@@G@@  ASG,NASG          . '@ASG,AI LOG$'@F@/@;CONT0     SZ        A5        OX
)@@G@@        . ASSIGN LATEST LOG CYCLE   @F@@@/CONT1     SZ        A5        OY
)@@G@@        . ASSIGN LATEST LOG CYCLE   @ @@@;          L,U       A6,' '    OZ
)@@G@@@ @@@;          SLJ       CYCLE     @D@@@9          MSCON$    MSCONPKT  PA
)@@G@@        . GET LEAD ITEM @H@@@9                                      . CHPB
)@@G@@ANGE MSCON PKT TO READ MAIN ITEM    @E@@@9          SP1,S3    MSCONPKT+3PC
)@@G@@        .   FOR LATER CALLS   @G@@@9          L,S4      A0,BUFFER+9     PD
)@@G@@  . CALCULATE OLDEST REL CYCLE-1    @^@@@9          A,U       A0,1@C@@@9PE
)@@G@@          SN        A0,LOGCYCLE       . STORE   @E@9@8CONT0     LMJ     PF
)@@G@@  X11,NEXT          . GET NEXT LOG CYCLE  @E@/@9CONT1     LMJ       X9,NPG
)@@G@@EXT           . GET NEXT LOG CYCLE  @E@@@/          LMJ       X9,NEXT   PH
)@@G@@        . GET NEXT LOG CYCLE  @C@@@8          J         EXIT            PI
)@@G@@  . ERROR   @F@9@8CONT1     LMJ       X11,READ          . READ NEXT MASTPJ
)@@G@@ER LOG BLOCK@F@@@9CONT2     LMJ       X9,READ           . READ NEXT MASTPK
)@@G@@ER LOG BLOCK@F@@@8          L         A0,0,X5           . CHECK FOR END PL
)@@G@@OF CYCLE    @ @@@8          TNE       A0,(-0)   @C@9@8          J       PM
)@@G@@  CONT7             . YES     @C@@@9          J         CONT11          PN
)@@G@@  . YES     @H@@@8          TE        A0,SENTINEL       . CHECK FOR LASTPO
)@@G@@ TAPE BLOCK SENTINEL    @^@@@8          J         $+3 @G@9@8          SZPP
)@@G@@        FIRST             . INITIALIZE FIRST TIME THRU FLAG @F@@@9      PQ
)@@G@@    SZ        FIRST             . CLEAR FIRST TIME THRU FLAG@D@@@8      PR
)@@G@@    J         EXIT              . END OF TAPE   @G@@@8          L       PS
)@@G@@  A0,STIME          . CHECK STARTING TIME IF SPECIFIED@ @9@8          JZPT
)@@G@@        A0,CONT2  @ @@@9          JZ        A0,CONT3  @D@@@8          L PU
)@@G@@        A1,LLOGT          . GET LOG TIME  @E@@@8          SLJ       DTDAPV
)@@G@@TE            . COMPARE WITH STIME  @G@9@8          AU        A2,60*60  PW
)@@G@@        . IF STIME MORE THAN 1 HOUR IN    @G@@@9          AU,U      A2,6PX
)@@G@@0*60          . IF STIME MORE THAN 1 HOUR IN    @G@@@8          TP      PY
)@@G@@  A3                .   FUTURE, SKIP REST OF BLOCK    @G@9@8          SZPZ
)@@G@@        NBUF              . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @G@@@9      QA
)@@G@@    SZ        ENTRYNUM          . NOT EQUAL, SKIP WHOLE BLOCK     @F@9@8QB
)@@G@@          JN        A2,CONT1          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @F@@@9QC
)@@G@@          JN        A2,CONT2          . JUMP IF STIME IN FUTURE?  @E@@@9QD
)@@G@@CONT3     TZ        PRIV              . IS RUN PRIVILEGED?  @C@@@9      QE
)@@G@@    J         CONT4             . YES     @F@@@9          L         A0,(QF
)@@G@@'EXEC 8')     . NO, SKIP EXEC 8 ENTRIES   @ @@@9          TNE       A0,LQG
)@@G@@RUNID @ @@@9          J         CONT2     @F@9@8CONT2     L         A0,RQH
)@@G@@UNID          . CHECK RUNID IF SPECIFIED, @F@@@9CONT4     L         A0,RQI
)@@G@@UNID          . CHECK RUNID IF SPECIFIED, @G@9@8          JZ        A0,CQJ
)@@G@@ONT4          .    IGNORING '-'S IN INPUT RUNID @G@@@9          JZ      QK
)@@G@@  A0,CONT7          .    IGNORING '-'S IN INPUT RUNID @^@@@8          L,QL
)@@G@@U       X4,5@ @9@8CONT2A    EX        LOAD,X4   @ @@@9CONT5     EX      QM
)@@G@@  LOAD,X4   @ @@@8          TNE,U     A0,'-'    @ @9@8          J       QN
)@@G@@  CONT3     @ @@@9          J         CONT6     @ @@@8          EX      QO
)@@G@@  TEST,X4   @ @9@8          J         CONT3     @ @@@9          J       QP
)@@G@@  CONT6     @^@9@8          SZ        NBUF@ @@@9          SZ        ENTRQQ
)@@G@@YNUM  @ @9@8          J         CONT1     @ @@@9          J         CONTQR
)@@G@@2     @ @9@8CONT3     JGD       X4,CONT2A @ @@@9CONT6     JGD       X4,CQS
)@@G@@ONT5  @F@9@8CONT4     L         A1,TYPE           . CHECK TYPE IF SPECIFQT
)@@G@@IED   @F@@@9CONT7     L         A1,TYPE           . CHECK TYPE IF SPECIFQU
)@@G@@IED   @ @@@8          L,H2      A0,0,A1   @F@@@8          TNZ,H1    0,X1QV
)@@G@@0             . CHECK IF TYPE TABLE INPUT @E@9@8          J         CONTQW
)@@G@@4A            . NO, JUST ONE TYPE   @E@@@9          J         CONT8     QX
)@@G@@        . NO, JUST ONE TYPE   @F@@@8          L,H1      R1,0,X10        QY
)@@G@@  . SCAN TYPE TABLE FOR MATCH @ @@@8          L         X1,0,X10  @^@@@8QZ
)@@G@@          LXI,U     X1,1@ @@@8          L         A0,LTYPE  @ @@@8      RA
)@@G@@    SE,H2     A0,0,*X1  @E@9@8          J         CONT1             . NORB
)@@G@@ FIND, SKIP ENTRY @E@@@9          J         CONT2             . NO FIND,RC
)@@G@@ SKIP ENTRY @F@9@8          J         CONT5             . TYPE MATCHES, RD
)@@G@@PROCESS     @F@@@9          J         CONT9             . TYPE MATCHES, RE
)@@G@@PROCESS     @E@9@8CONT4A    JZ        A0,CONT5          . NO TYPE SPECIFRF
)@@G@@IED   @E@@@9CONT8     JZ        A0,CONT9          . NO TYPE SPECIFIED   RG
)@@G@@@ @@@8          TE        A0,LTYPE  @ @9@8          J         CONT1     RH
)@@G@@@ @@@9          J         CONT2     @G@9@8CONT5     L         A0,KEY    RI
)@@G@@        . CHECK SEARCH KEY IF SPECIFIED   @G@@@9CONT9     L         A0,KRJ
)@@G@@EY            . CHECK SEARCH KEY IF SPECIFIED   @ @9@8          JZ      RK
)@@G@@  A0,CONT6  @ @@@9          JZ        A0,CONT10 @D@@@9          TZ      RL
)@@G@@  WDNO              . IS WORD # = 0?@G@@@9          J         CONT9A    RM
)@@G@@        . NO, PLAIN SEARCH KEY SPECIFIED  @G@@@9          L         X1,XRN
)@@G@@5             . YES, STRING SEARCH SPECIFIED    @ @@@9          L,H2    RO
)@@G@@  X2,3,X10  @ @@@9          L,U       A1,24*6   @^@@@9          L,U     RP
)@@G@@  A2,6@A@@@9          LMJ       X11,FINDFIELD   @E@@@9          J       RQ
)@@G@@  CONT2             . NO FIND, SKIP ENTRY @F@@@9          J         CONTRR
)@@G@@10            . STRING FOUND, CONTINUE    @ @9@8          L         X4,WRS
)@@G@@DNO   @ @@@9CONT9A    L         X4,WDNO   @ @@@8          A         X4,XRT
)@@G@@5     @ @@@8          L         A1,0,X4   @ @@@8          TE        A1,ARU
)@@G@@0     @ @9@8          J         CONT1     @ @@@9          J         CONTRV
)@@G@@2     @F@9@8CONT6     L,U       R1,28             . MOVE BUFFER TO USER'RW
)@@G@@S AREA@F@@@9CONT10    L,U       R1,28             . MOVE BUFFER TO USER'RX
)@@G@@S AREA@ @@@8          L,U       X4,BUFF   @^@@@8          LXI,U     X4,1RY
)@@G@@@ @@@8          L         X6,X5     @^@@@8          LXI,U     X6,1@ @@@8RZ
)@@G@@          BT        X4,0,*X6  @E@@@8          S         X5,POINTER      SA
)@@G@@  . SAME BLOCK POINTER  @C@@@8          J         EXIT              . RESB
)@@G@@TURN  @I@9@8CONT7     TNZ       PREASG            . IF OTHER THAN MASTERSC
)@@G@@ LOG FILE, FINISHED     @I@@@9CONT11    TNZ       PREASG            . IFSD
)@@G@@ OTHER THAN MASTER LOG FILE, FINISHED     @E@9@8          LMJ       X11,SE
)@@G@@NEXT          . GET NEXT LOG CYCLE  @E@@@9          LMJ       X9,NEXT   SF
)@@G@@        . GET NEXT LOG CYCLE  @H@@@8          J         EXIT            SG
)@@G@@  . ERROR - FINISHED SEARCH (NO FIND)     @C@9@8          J         CONTSH
)@@G@@1             . CONTINUE@C@@@9          J         CONT2             . COSI
)@@G@@NTINUE@F@@@8EXIT      TZ,S1     0,X10             . CHECK FOR FOR V OR FSJ
)@@G@@TN    @C@@@8          J         0,X10             . FTN     @C@@@8      SK
)@@G@@    J         6,X10             . FOR V   @[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. **********SL
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @H@@@8SM
)@@G@@. *******              READ LOG ENTRY SUBROUTINE                     ***SN
)@@G@@****  @H@@@8. **********************************************************SO
)@@G@@****************  @[@@@8.     @]@@@8READ      . @F@9@8          TZ      SP
)@@G@@  NBUF              . IS NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @F@@@9          TZ      SQ
)@@G@@  ENTRYNUM          . IS NO. OF BUFFERS = 0 ?   @B@@@8          J       SR
)@@G@@  READ3             . NO@I@@@8          L         A0,READP+5        . YESS
)@@G@@S, INCREMENT DRUM ADDRESS BY 8 SECTORS    @^@@@8          A,U       A0,8ST
)@@G@@@ @@@8READ1     S         A0,READP+5@F@@@8          IOW$      READP     SU
)@@G@@        . READ NEXT 224 WORD BLOCK  @ @@@8          TZ,S1     READP+3   SV
)@@G@@@C@@@8          J         READE             . ERROR   @F@@@9          INSW
)@@G@@C       NBLOCKS           . INCREMENT BLOCK COUNT     @#@@@9          NOSX
)@@G@@P     @E@@@8          L         A0,('SYSLOG')     . LOG FILE HEADER ?   SY
)@@G@@@ @@@8          TE        A0,BUFFER @B@@@8          J         READ2     SZ
)@@G@@        . NO@G@@@8          L         A0,BUFFER+2       . YES, GET SECTOTA
)@@G@@R ADDRESS OF DATA @G@@@9          A         A0,READP+5        . ADD TO PTB
)@@G@@RESENT SECTOR ADDRESS   @G@@@8          J         READ1             . GOTC
)@@G@@ BACK AND READ THAT SECTOR    @F@@@8READ2     L,S6      A0,BUFFER       TD
)@@G@@  . SET MAX NO. OF BUFFERS    @G@@@8          JZ        A0,READ         TE
)@@G@@  . SKIP BLOCKS WITH NO ENTRIES     @ @@@8          S         A0,MNBUF  TF
)@@G@@@F@9@8          L,U       A0,1              . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAGTG
)@@G@@@F@@@9          SP1       NEWBLOCK          . SET NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TAGTH
)@@G@@@A@9@8          S         A0,NEWBLOCK     @^@@@8          J         $+2 TI
)@@G@@@G@@@8READ3     SZ        NEWBLOCK          . CLEAR NEW BLOCK EXTERNAL TTJ
)@@G@@AG    @F@9@8          L         A0,NBUF           . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFTK
)@@G@@FERS  @F@@@9          L         A0,ENTRYNUM       . INCREMENT NO. OF BUFTL
)@@G@@FERS  @^@@@8          AU,U      A0,1@ @@@8          MSI,U     A0,28     TM
)@@G@@@ @@@8          A,U       A0,BUFFER @ @@@8          S         A0,X5     TN
)@@G@@@F@@@8          TG        A1,MNBUF          . IF = MNBUF, RESET TO 0    TO
)@@G@@@^@@@8          SZ        A1  @ @9@8          S         A1,NBUF   @A@@@9TP
)@@G@@          S         A1,ENTRYNUM     @C@9@8          J         0,X11     TQ
)@@G@@        . RETURN  @F@@@9          INC       NRECS             . INCREMENTR
)@@G@@T NO. OF RECORDS  @#@@@9          NOP     @C@@@9          J         0,X9TS
)@@G@@              . RETURN  @F@@@8READE     .                           . CLTT
)@@G@@EAN END-OF-FILE CHECK   @E@@@8          L,S1      A0,READP+3        . CHTU
)@@G@@ECK FOR 1ST EOF   @^@@@8          TE,U      A0,1@F@@@8          J       TV
)@@G@@  EXIT              . NOT EOF, OTHER I/O ERROR  @E@@@8          IOW$    TW
)@@G@@  READP             . READ NEXT RECORD    @D@@@8          TZ,S1     READTX
)@@G@@P+3           . I/O ERROR?    @F@@@8          J         EXIT            TY
)@@G@@  . YES, PROBABLY DOUBLE EOF  @F@@@8          L,H2      A0,READP+3      TZ
)@@G@@  . CHECK IF 14 WD BUFFER READ@ @@@8          TE,U      A0,14     @E@@@8UA
)@@G@@          J         EXIT              . NO, GARBAGE READ    @G@@@8      UB
)@@G@@    L         A0,(0541600000000) . CHECK FOR END-OF-TAPE SDF LABEL@ @@@8UC
)@@G@@          TE        A0,BUFFER @E@@@8          J         EXIT            UD
)@@G@@  . NO, GARBAGE READ    @G@@@8          TSWAP$    FACPKT            . CLUE
)@@G@@EAN END-OF-REEL, SWAP TAPES   @^@@@8          J         READ@[@@@8/.    UF
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ****************************************************************UG
)@@G@@**********  @H@@@8. **********           GET NEXT LOG CYCLE SUBROUTINE  UH
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ****************************************UI
)@@G@@**********************************  @[@@@8.     @]@@@8NEXT      . @D@9@8UJ
)@@G@@          CSF$      FREE,NFREE        . @FREE MASTER  @D@@@9          CSUK
)@@G@@F$      FREE,NFREE        . @FREE LOG$    @E@9@8          L,S3      A1,CUL
)@@G@@YCLE          . IS CYCLE = -0 ?     @E@@@9NEXTA     INC       LOGCYCLE  UM
)@@G@@        . INCREMENT LOGCYCLE  @D@9@8NEXTA     TNE,U     A1,'0'          UN
)@@G@@  . IF SO, ERROR  @F@@@9          J         0,X9              . IF LOGCYUO
)@@G@@CLE WAS 0, ERROR  @ @9@8          J         0,X11     @D@9@8          ANUP
)@@G@@,U      A1,1              . UPDATE CYCLE  @ @9@8          S,S3      A1,CUQ
)@@G@@YCLE  @E@'@9          E$DIT     EPKT              . GENERATE USE IMAGE  UR
)@@G@@@^@'@9          E$MSG     USE @A@'@9          L         A0,LOGCYCLE     US
)@@G@@@A@@@'          L         A5,LOGCYCLE     @^@'@9          A,U       A0,1UT
)@@G@@@^@@@'          A,U       A5,1@ @@@'          L,U       A6,' '    @E@@@'UU
)@@G@@          SLJ       CYCLE             . ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE   @#@;@9      UV
)@@G@@    E$DECV  @#@;@9          E$MSGR  @G@9@8          CSF$      USE,NUSE  UW
)@@G@@        . @USE MASTER,SYS$*SYSTEM$...     @F@;@9          CSF$      BUFFUX
)@@G@@ER+28,14      . @USE LOG$,SYS$*SYSTEM$... @D@9@8          CSF$      ASG,UY
)@@G@@NASG          . @ASG,A MASTER @D@;@9          CSF$      ASG,NASG        UZ
)@@G@@  . @ASG,A LOG$   @E@@@8          JN        A0,NEXTA          . NG, TRY VA
)@@G@@NEXT CYCLE  @H@@@9          TNZ       PRINTCYCLE        . DOES USER WANTVB
)@@G@@ MASTER LOG SUMMARY?    @B@@@9          J         NEXTB             . NOVC
)@@G@@@G@@@9          MSCON$    MSCONPKT          . YES, GET MAIN ITEM FOR LOGVD
)@@G@@ FILE @E@@@9          E$DIT     EPKT              . INITIATE EDITOR     VE
)@@G@@@D@@@9          E$FD2     BUFFER+1          . QUALIFIER     @^@@@9      VF
)@@G@@    E$CHAR    '*' @D@@@9          E$FD2     BUFFER+3          . FILE-NAMVG
)@@G@@E     @^@@@9          E$CHAR    '(' @D@@@9          E$DECV    BUFFER+17,VH
)@@G@@,T3     . ABS CYCLE     @^@@@9          E$MSG     MESS@A@@@9          L VI
)@@G@@        A0,LOGCYCLE     @^@@@9          A,U       A0,1@D@@@9          E$VJ
)@@G@@DECV                      . REL CYCLE     @#@@@9          E$MSGR  @E@@@9VK
)@@G@@          E$DAY3    BUFFER+19         . CATALOGUE TDATE     @^@@@9      VL
)@@G@@    E$SKIP    1   @ @@@9          E$TIME    BUFFER+19 @D@@@9          PRVM
)@@G@@INT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   @E@@@9          E$PRINT       VN
)@@G@@              . PRINT SUMMARY LINE  @D@@@9          PRINT$    0,0,1     VO
)@@G@@        . SKIP A LINE   @G@@@'NEXTB     TNZ       STIME             . WAVP
)@@G@@S A START TIME SPECIFIED?     @B@;@'          J         NEXTX           VQ
)@@G@@  . NO@B@@@;          J         NEXTC             . NO@F@@@'          A,VR
)@@G@@U       A5,1              . YES, ASSIGN NEXT CYCLE +1 @E@@@'          L,VS
)@@G@@U       A6,'1'            .   FOR LOOK AHEAD    @ @@@'          SLJ     VT
)@@G@@  CYCLE     @H@@@'          JN        A0,NEXTC          . PROBLEM WITH TVU
)@@G@@HAT CYCLE, FORGET IT    @F@@@'          MSCON$    MSCONPKT1         . GEVV
)@@G@@T MAIN ITEM OF CYCLE    @G@@@'          L         A0,STIME          . COVW
)@@G@@MPARE START TIME WITH CYCLE'S @E@@@'          L         A1,BUFFER+19    VX
)@@G@@  .    CATALOGUE TIME   @H@@@'          SLJ       DTDATE            . IFVY
)@@G@@ START TIME > CATALOGUE TIME, SKIP  @E@;@'          JN        A2,NEXTA  VZ
)@@G@@        .    PRESENT CYCLE    @E@@@;          JN        A2,NEXT         WA
)@@G@@  .    PRESENT CYCLE    @F@9@8          LN,U      A0,8              . INWB
)@@G@@ITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   @F@'@9NEXTB     LN,U      A0,8              . INWC
)@@G@@ITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   @F@@@'NEXTC     LN,U      A0,8              . INWD
)@@G@@ITIALIZE DRUM ADDRESS   @ @@@8          S         A0,READP+5@G@9@8      WE
)@@G@@    SZ        NBUF              . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   @G@@@9WF
)@@G@@          SZ        ENTRYNUM          . INIT. NO. OF BUFFERS FOR READ   WG
)@@G@@@C@9@8          J         1,X11             . RETURN  @C@@@9          J WH
)@@G@@        1,X9              . RETURN  @[@@@'/.    @H@@@'. ****************WI
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @H@@@'. ****WJ
)@@G@@*** ASSIGN LOG CYCLE SUBROUTINE                                *******  WK
)@@G@@@H@@@'. *******                                                         WL
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@'. ******* INPUTS: A5 = REL CYCLE                      WM
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@'. *******         A6 = LOG$ SUFFIX        WN
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@'. *******                     WO
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@'. ****************WP
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @^@@@'CYCLE WQ
)@@G@@    +         0   @E@@@'          E$DIT     EPKT              . EDIT 'USWR
)@@G@@E' IMAGE    @D@@@'          E$MSG     USE               . '@USE LOG$&'  WS
)@@G@@@D@@@'          E$FD1     A6                . LOG$ SUFFIX   @C@@@'      WT
)@@G@@    E$MSGR                      . ',(&'   @D@@@'          E$DECV    A5  WU
)@@G@@              . REL CYCLE     @ @@@'          E$MSGR    . ')'     @E@@@'WV
)@@G@@          CSF$      BUFFER+28,14      . SUBMIT USE IMAGE    @E@@@'      WW
)@@G@@    E$DIT     EPKT              . EDIT 'ASG' IMAGE    @E@@@'          E$WX
)@@G@@MSG     ASG               . '@ASG,AI LOG$&'     @D@@@'          E$FD1   WY
)@@G@@  A6                . LOG$ SUFFIX   @E@@@'          CSF$      BUFFER+28,WZ
)@@G@@14      . SUBMIT ASG IMAGE    @C@@@'          J         *CYCLE          XA
)@@G@@  . RETURN  @[@@@'.     @[@@@8/.    @H@@@8. ****************************XB
)@@G@@*********************************************** @H@@@8. *******         XC
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@8. ****XD
)@@G@@*** TDATE TIME DIFFERENCE SUBROUTINE                           *******  XE
)@@G@@@H@@@8. *******                                                         XF
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. ******* WRITTEN BY LOU INFELD, 10/07/77             XG
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. *******                                 XH
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@8. ******* THIS SUBROUTINE WILLXI
)@@G@@ CALCULATE THE TIME DIFFERENCE         *******  @H@@@8. ******* IN SECONXJ
)@@G@@DS BETWEEN TWO TIMES EXPRESSED IN 'TDATE$' FORMAT. *******  @H@@@8. ****XK
)@@G@@***                                                            *******  XL
)@@G@@@H@@@8. ******* INPUTS ARE IN A0 & A1 AND OUTPUT IS IN A2.  A2=A1-A0.   XM
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@8. *******                                             XN
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@8. ****************************************XO
)@@G@@************************************@#@@@8$(1)      AXR$    @E@@@8DTDATEXP
)@@G@@*   +         0                 . 'SLJ DTDATE' CALL   @D@@@8          DSXQ
)@@G@@        A0,DTDIN          . SAVE INPUT    @H@@@8          L,H1      A2,DXR
)@@G@@TDIN          . CHECK IF MMDDYY SAME FOR BOTH TIMES   @ @@@8          TEXS
)@@G@@,H1     A2,DTDIN+1@D@@@8          J         DTDCON1           . NO, TOO XT
)@@G@@BAD   @F@@@8          L         A2,A1             . YES, EASY CALCULATIOXU
)@@G@@N     @ @@@8          AN        A2,A0     @C@@@8          J         *DTDXV
)@@G@@ATE           . ALL DONE@G@@@8DTDCON1   SLJ       DTDSUB            . COXW
)@@G@@NVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964, D.P.@E@@@8          S         A0,DTDTEMP      XX
)@@G@@  . SAVE CONVERTED TIME @ @@@8          L         A0,DTDIN+1@G@@@8      XY
)@@G@@    SLJ       DTDSUB            . CONVERT TO SECS SINCE 1964, D.P.@E@@@8XZ
)@@G@@          AN        A0,DTDTEMP        . CALCULATE DIFFERENCE@E@@@8      YA
)@@G@@    L         A2,A0             . GET OUTPUT READY    @D@@@8          DLYB
)@@G@@        A0,DTDIN          . RESTORE INPUT @C@@@8          J         *DTDYC
)@@G@@ATE           . DONE    @H@@@8. ****************************************YD
)@@G@@**********************************  @H@@@8. ********* CONVERT TDATE$ TO YE
)@@G@@SECONDS SINCE 1964                     *******  @H@@@8. ****************YF
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @^@@@8DTDSUBYG
)@@G@@    +         0   @D@@@8          S         A0,DTDTEMP+1      . SAVE INPYH
)@@G@@UT    @^@@@8          SZ        A2  @C@@@8          L,S3      A3,DTDTEMPYI
)@@G@@+1      . YEAR    @ @@@8          JZ        A3,DTDSC1 @^@@@8          ANYJ
)@@G@@,U      A3,1@ @@@8          L         A0,A3     @E@@@8          DI,U    YK
)@@G@@  A2,4              . CHECK FOR LEAP YEARS@^@@@8          A,U       A2,1YL
)@@G@@@A@@@8          MSI,U     A2,60*60*24     @B@@@8          MSI       A0,(YM
)@@G@@60*60*24*365)     @ @@@8          A         A0,A2     @C@@@8DTDSC1    L,YN
)@@G@@S1      A2,DTDTEMP+1      . MONTH   @^@@@8          AN,U      A2,1@A@@@8YO

)@@G@@,U      A2,1@E@@@8          MSI,U     A2,60*60*24       . CONVERT TO SECYR
)@@G@@S     @D@@@8          A         A0,A2             . ADD TO TOTAL  @G@@@8YS
)@@G@@          L,S3      A3,DTDTEMP+1       . IF LEAP YEAR AND MONTH>FEB,    YT
)@@G@@@H@@@8          AND,U     A3,3              .    ADD AN EXTRA DAY TO CALYU
)@@G@@CULATION    @ @@@8          JNZ       A4,DTDSC3 @A@@@8          L,S1    YV
)@@G@@  A3,DTDTEMP+1    @^@@@8          TLE,U     A3,3@ @@@8          J       YW
)@@G@@  DTDSC3    @A@@@8          A,U       A0,60*60*24     @C@@@8DTDSC3    L,YX
)@@G@@H2      A2,DTDTEMP+1      . SECS    @D@@@8          A         A0,A2     YY
)@@G@@        . ADD TO TOTAL  @C@@@8          J         *DTDSUB           . REYZ
)@@G@@TURN  @C@9@8DTDIN     RES       2                 . INPUT   @C@@@9DTDIN ZA
)@@G@@    $RES      2                 . INPUT   @^@9@8DTDTEMP   RES       2   ZB

)@@G@@        60*60*24*30     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*31     @A@@@8ZG

)@@G@@0     @A@@@8          +         60*60*24*31     @A@@@8          +       ZI

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******         A1 - NUMBER OF BYTES IN BLOCK       DS
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. *******         A2 - NUMBER OF BYTES IN DT
)@@G@@FIELD                      *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUTPUT: A0 - BYTE # DU
)@@G@@IN BLOCK WHERE FIELD FOUND             *******  @H@@@C. *******         DV
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@C. ****DW
)@@G@@*** CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,FINDFIELD                        *******  DX
)@@G@@@H@@@C. *******                     J NOFIND                            DY
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J FIND                  DZ
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@C. *******                                 EA
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@C. ****************************EB
)@@G@@**********************************************  @]@@@CFINDFIELD*  @E@@@CEC
)@@G@@          S         X11,SAVE+2        . SAVE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C      ED
)@@G@@    DS        A1,SAVE+3 @ @@@C          S         X1,SAVE+5 @H@@@C      EE
)@@G@@    AN        A1,A2             . CALC # OF TIMES TO COMPARE FIELDS     EF
)@@G@@@ @@@C          S         A1,R1     @ @@@C          L         A0,A2     EG
)@@G@@@E@@@C          LMJ       X11,BCOMP         . COMPARE 2 FIELDS    @D@@@CEH
)@@G@@          JZ        A0,FINDF          . FIELD FOUND   @E@@@C          A EI
)@@G@@        X1,(1,0)          . BUMP BYTE # OF BLOCK@F@@@C          JGD     EJ
)@@G@@  R1,$-4            . CHECK FOR END OF BLOCK    @G@@@C          J       EK
)@@G@@  FINDN             . END OF BLOCK, FIELD NOT FOUND   @G@@@CFINDF     L EL
)@@G@@        A0,X1             . GET BYTE # WHERE FIELD FOUND    @ @@@C      EM
)@@G@@    SSL       A0,18     @D@@@C          L         X11,SAVE+2        . REEN
)@@G@@STORE X11   @F@@@C          A,U       X11,1             . POINT TO NORMAEO
)@@G@@L RETURN    @D@@@C          J         $+2               . NORMAL RETURN EP
)@@G@@@D@@@CFINDN     L         X11,SAVE+2        . RESTORE X11   @ @@@C      EQ
)@@G@@    DL        A1,SAVE+3 @ @@@C          L         X1,SAVE+5 @C@@@C      ER
)@@G@@    J         0,X11             . RETURN  @[@@@C.     @H@@@C. **********ES
)@@G@@****************************************************************  @H@@@CET
)@@G@@. ******* CONVERT TIME/DATE STRING TO TDATE$ FORMAT SUBROUTINE       ***EU
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. ******* (STRINGS CAN BE OF FORM: 'HH:MM:SS' OR 'MM/DD/YY')EV
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. *******                                       EW
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. ******* INPUT:  X1 - (BYTE #,INPUTEX
)@@G@@ BASE ADDRESS)                   *******  @H@@@C. *******         R1 - #EY
)@@G@@ OF BYTES IN INPUT STRING                    *******  @H@@@C. ******* OUEZ
)@@G@@TPUT: A0 - TDATE$ WORD                                   *******  @H@@@CFA
)@@G@@. *******         A1 - BYTE # AFTER FIELD                            ***FB
)@@G@@****  @H@@@C. *******                                                   FC
)@@G@@         *******  @H@@@C. ******* CALLING SEQUENCE: LMJ X11,BTDATE      FD
)@@G@@                     *******  @H@@@C. *******                     J ERROFE
)@@G@@R                                *******  @H@@@C. *******               FF
)@@G@@      J NORMAL                               *******  @H@@@C. *******   FG
)@@G@@                                                         *******  @H@@@CFH
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************FI
)@@G@@****  @]@@@CBTDATE*     @E@@@C          S         X11,10            . SAFJ
)@@G@@VE REGISTERS USED @ @@@C          S         X1,SBTDATE@A@@@C          DSFK
)@@G@@        A1,SBTDATE+1    @A@@@C          S         X2,SBTDATE+3    @A@@@CFL
)@@G@@          S         A3,SBTDATE+4    @D@@@C          L         A0,BASCII FM
)@@G@@        . ASCII KEY     @G@@@C          LSSL      A0,18             . SHFN
)@@G@@IFT H1 TO H2 FOR GETFIELD     @ @@@C          S         A0,BASCII @D@@@CFO
)@@G@@          SZ        TDATEA            . CLEAR OUTPUT  @E@@@C          L,FP
)@@G@@U       X2,BUFF           . EXTRACT NEXT FIELD  @^@@@C          L,U     FQ
)@@G@@  R2,8@A@@@C          LMJ       X11,GETFIELD    @D@@@C          J       FR
)@@G@@  BTDATEE+1         . NO MORE FIELDS@F@@@C          A         A0,A1     FS
)@@G@@        . CALC BYTE # AFTER FIELD   @C@@@C          S         A0,SBTDATEFT
)@@G@@+1      . SAVE    @F@@@C          L,U       A0,'/'            . IS FIELDFU
)@@G@@ DATE OR TIME?    @ @@@C          TE,S3     A0,BUFF   @C@@@C          J FV
)@@G@@        TDATET            . TIME    @D@@@C          TE,S6     A0,BUFF   FW
)@@G@@        . CHECK FORMAT  @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . FOFX
)@@G@@RMAT ERROR  @^@@@C          L,U       A2,0@ @@@C          L,U       A3,1FY
)@@G@@2     @D@@@C          L,S1      A0,BUFF           . CONVERT 'MM'  @ @@@CFZ
)@@G@@          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@CGA
)@@G@@          L,S2      A1,BUFF   @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@CGB
)@@G@@          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0           GC
)@@G@@  . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1       GD
)@@G@@  . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C          S,S1      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOGE
)@@G@@R OUTPUT    @ @@@C          L,U       A3,31     @D@@@C          L,S4    GF
)@@G@@  A0,BUFF           . CONVERT 'DD'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    GG
)@@G@@@ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S5      A1,BUFF   GH
)@@G@@@ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,A1     GI
)@@G@@@F@@@C          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    GJ
)@@G@@@D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C      GK
)@@G@@    S,S2      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @ @@@C          L,GL
)@@G@@U       A2,64     @ @@@C          L,U       A3,99     @D@@@C          L,GM
)@@G@@S1      A0,BUFF+1         . CONVERT 'YY'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'GN
)@@G@@0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S2      A1,BGO
)@@G@@UFF+1 @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,AGP
)@@G@@1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMIGQ
)@@G@@TS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @D@@@CGR
)@@G@@          AN,U      A0,64             . MODULO 64     @E@@@C          S,GS
)@@G@@S3      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @D@@@C          L       GT
)@@G@@  A0,TDATEA         . GET OUTPUT    @C@@@C          J         BTDATEE   GU
)@@G@@        . RETURN  @F@@@CTDATET    L,U       A0,':'            . CHECK FOGV
)@@G@@R FORMAT ERROR    @ @@@C          TE,S3     A0,BUFF   @D@@@C          J GW
)@@G@@        BTDATEE+1         . FORMAT ERROR  @ @@@C          TE,S6     A0,BGX
)@@G@@UFF   @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . FORMAT ERROR  @^@@@CGY
)@@G@@          LN,U      A2,1@ @@@C          L,U       A3,23     @D@@@C      GZ
)@@G@@    L,S1      A0,BUFF           . CONVERT 'HH'  @ @@@C          AN,U    HA
)@@G@@  A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSI,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S2    HB
)@@G@@  A1,BUFF   @ @@@C          AN,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A       HC
)@@G@@  A0,A1     @F@@@C          TW        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIHD
)@@G@@N LIMITS    @D@@@C          J         BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     HE
)@@G@@@E@@@C          S,S1      A0,TDATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @ @@@CHF
)@@G@@          L,U       A3,59     @D@@@C          L,S4      A0,BUFF         HG
)@@G@@  . CONVERT 'MM'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C          MSHH
)@@G@@I,U     A0,10     @ @@@C          L,S5      A1,BUFF   @ @@@C          ANHI
)@@G@@,U      A1,'0'    @ @@@C          A         A0,A1     @F@@@C          TWHJ
)@@G@@        A2,A0             . CHECK IF WITHIN LIMITS    @D@@@C          J HK
)@@G@@        BTDATEE+1         . NO, ERROR     @E@@@C          S,S2      A0,THL
)@@G@@DATEA         . STORE FOR OUTPUT    @D@@@C          L,S1      A0,BUFF+1 HM
)@@G@@        . CONVERT 'SS'  @ @@@C          AN,U      A0,'0'    @ @@@C      HN
